Section BiadjunctionPreservation.
  Context {B₁ B₂ : bicat}
          {L : psfunctor B₁ B₂}
          (R : left_biadj_data L).

  Section PreserveEquifiers.
    Context {y₁ y₂ : B₂}
            {f g : y₁ --> y₂}
            {α β : f ==> g}
            {e : equifier_cone f g α β}
            (He : has_equifier_ump e).

biadj_unit R x · # R h ◃ ## R β

    Qed.

    Definition right_biadj_preserves_equifiers_nat_trans_cell
               {x : B₁}
               (h : x --> R e)
      : biadj_unit R x · # R (# L h · biadj_counit R e · equifier_cone_pr1 e)
        ==>
        h · # R (equifier_cone_pr1 e)
      := (_ ◃ ((psfunctor_comp R _ _)^-1
               • ((psfunctor_comp R _ _)^-1 ▹ _)))
         • lassociator _ _ _
         • (lassociator _ _ _ ▹ _)
         • (((psnaturality_of (biadj_unit R) h) ▹ _) ▹ _)
         • rassociator _ _ _
         • rassociator _ _ _
         • (_ ◃ (lassociator _ _ _
                 • ((linvunitor _
                 • (_ ◃ (_ ◃ (linvunitor _ • (_ ◃ rinvunitor _))))
                 • invertible_modcomponent_of (biadj_triangle_r R) e) ▹ _)
                 • lunitor _)).

    Definition right_biadj_preserves_equifiers_commute_data
               (x : B₁)
      : nat_trans_data
          (biadj_left_hom R x e
           ∙ to_universal_equifier_cat e (L x)
           ∙ full_sub_category_functor
               (λ (h : hom (L x) y₁),
                make_hProp
                  (h ◃ α = h ◃ β)
                  (cellset_property _ _ _ _))
               (λ (h : hom x (R y₁)),
                make_hProp
                  (h ◃ ## R α = h ◃ ## R β)
                  (cellset_property _ _ _ _))
               (biadj_right_hom R x y₁)
               preserve_equifiers_R_path)
          (to_universal_equifier_cat (psfunctor_equifier_cone R e) x)
      := λ h, right_biadj_preserves_equifiers_nat_trans_cell h ,, tt.

    
B₁, B₂: bicat
L: psfunctor B₁ B₂
R: left_biadj_data L
y₁, y₂: B₂
f, g: B₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
α, β: f ==> g
e: equifier_cone f g α β
He: has_equifier_ump e
x: B₁
is_nat_trans
  ((biadj_left_hom R x e
    ∙ to_universal_equifier_cat e (L x))
   ∙ full_sub_category_functor
       (λ h : hom (L x) y₁,
        make_hProp (h ◃ α = h ◃ β)
          (cellset_property (h · f) (h · g) (h ◃ α)
             (h ◃ β)))
       (λ h : hom x (R y₁),
        make_hProp (h ◃ ## R α = h ◃ ## R β)
          (cellset_property (h · # R f) (h · # R g)
             (h ◃ ## R α) (h ◃ ## R β)))
       (biadj_right_hom R x y₁)
       preserve_equifiers_R_path)
  (to_universal_equifier_cat
     (psfunctor_equifier_cone R e) x)
  (right_biadj_preserves_equifiers_commute_data x)

L: psfunctor B₁ B₂
R: left_biadj_data L
y₁, y₂: B₂
f, g: B₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧

He: has_equifier_ump e
x: B₁
h₁, h₂: hom x (R e)
ζ: hom x (R e) ⟦ h₁, h₂ ⟧
# ((biadj_left_hom R x e
    ∙ to_universal_equifier_cat e (L x))
   ∙ full_sub_category_functor
       (λ h : hom (L x) y₁,
        make_hProp (h ◃ α = h ◃ β)
          (cellset_property (h · f) (h · g) (h ◃ α)
             (h ◃ β)))
       (λ h : hom x (R y₁),
        make_hProp (h ◃ ## R α = h ◃ ## R β)
          (cellset_property (h · # R f) (h · # R g)
             (h ◃ ## R α) (h ◃ ## R β)))
       (biadj_right_hom R x y₁)
       preserve_equifiers_R_path) ζ
· right_biadj_preserves_equifiers_commute_data x h₂ =
right_biadj_preserves_equifiers_commute_data x h₁
· # (to_universal_equifier_cat
       (psfunctor_equifier_cone R e) x) ζ

              (h ◃ ## R α) (h ◃ ## R β))))

          ◃ (linvunitor
               ((pr111 (Whiskering.right_whisker
                          (pr1 R) (biadj_unit (pr1 R))))
                  e
                · (pr111 (Whiskering.left_whisker
                            (pr1 R)
                            (biadj_counit (pr1 R)))) e)
             ▹ # R (equifier_cone_pr1 e)))
         • (# (id_psfunctor B₁) h₁
            ◃ (((id₁ (pr1 R e)
                 ◃ ((pr111 (Whiskering.right_whisker
                              (...) (...))) e
                    ◃ linvunitor ((pr111 (...)) e)))
                • (id₁ (pr1 R e)
                   ◃ ((pr111 (Whiskering.right_whisker
                                (...) (...))) e
                      ◃ (id₁ (... e)
                         ◃ rinvunitor (... e)))))
               ▹ # R (equifier_cone_pr1 e))))
        • (# (id_psfunctor B₁) h₁
           ◃ (invertible_modcomponent_of
                (biadj_triangle_r R) e
              ▹ # R (equifier_cone_pr1 e)))))
    • (# (id_psfunctor B₁) h₁
       ◃ lunitor (# R (equifier_cone_pr1 e)))))
• (ζ ▹ # R (equifier_cone_pr1 e))

f, g: B₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
α, β: f ==> g
e: equifier_cone f g α β
He: has_equifier_ump e
x: B₁
h₁, h₂: hom x (R e)
ζ: hom x (R e) ⟦ h₁, h₂ ⟧
?b =
(biadj_unit R x
 ◃ ((psfunctor_comp R (# L h₁)
       (biadj_counit (pr1 R) e)) ^-1
    ▹ # R (equifier_cone_pr1 e)))
• (lassociator (biadj_unit R x)
     (# R (# L h₁) · # R (biadj_counit (pr1 R) e))
     (# R (equifier_cone_pr1 e))
   • ((lassociator (biadj_unit R x) (# R (# L h₁))
         (# R (biadj_counit (pr1 R) e))
       ▹ # R (equifier_cone_pr1 e))
      • (((psnaturality_of (biadj_unit R) h₁
           ▹ # R (biadj_counit (pr1 R) e))
          ▹ # R (equifier_cone_pr1 e))
         • (rassociator
              (# (id_psfunctor B₁) h₁
               · biadj_unit R (R e))
              (# R (biadj_counit (pr1 R) e))
              (# R (equifier_cone_pr1 e))
            • (rassociator (# (id_psfunctor B₁) h₁)
                 (biadj_unit R (R e))
                 (# R (biadj_counit (pr1 R) e)
                  · # R (equifier_cone_pr1 e))
               • ((# (id_psfunctor B₁) h₁
                   ◃ lassociator
                       ((pr111 (Whiskering.right_whisker
                                  (pr1 R)
                                  (biadj_unit (pr1 R))))
                          e)
                       ((pr111 (Whiskering.left_whisker
                                  (pr1 R)
                                  (biadj_counit
                                     (pr1 R)))) e)
                       (# R (equifier_cone_pr1 e)))
                  • ((# (id_psfunctor B₁) h₁
                      ◃ (linvunitor
                           ((pr111 (Whiskering.right_whisker
                                      ... ...)) e
                            · (pr111 (Whiskering.left_whisker
                                        ... ...)) e)
                         ▹ # R (equifier_cone_pr1 e)))
                     • ((# (id_psfunctor B₁) h₁
                         ◃ (((id₁ ... ◃ (...))
                             • (id₁ ... ◃ (...)))
                            ▹ # R
                                (equifier_cone_pr1 e)))
                        • ((# (id_psfunctor B₁) h₁
                            ◃ (invertible_modcomponent_of
                                 (biadj_triangle_r R)
                                 e
                               ▹ # R
                                   (equifier_cone_pr1
                                      e)))
                           • ((# (id_psfunctor B₁) h₁
                               ◃ lunitor (# R ...))
                              • (ζ
                                 ▹ # R
                                     (equifier_cone_pr1
                                        e))))))))))))

              ▹ # R (biadj_counit (pr1 R) e))
             ▹ # R (equifier_cone_pr1 e))

                 (# (id_psfunctor B₁) h₂
                  · biadj_unit R (R e))

                 (# R (equifier_cone_pr1 e))
               • (rassociator (# (id_psfunctor B₁) h₂)
                    (biadj_unit R (R e))
                    (# R (biadj_counit (pr1 R) e)
                     · # R (equifier_cone_pr1 e))
                  • ((# (id_psfunctor B₁) h₂
                      ◃ lassociator
                          ((pr111 (Whiskering.right_whisker
                                     (pr1 R)
                                     (biadj_unit (...))))
                             e)
                          ((pr111 (Whiskering.left_whisker
                                     (pr1 R)
                                     (biadj_counit
                                        (...)))) e)
                          (# R (equifier_cone_pr1 e)))
                     • ((# (id_psfunctor B₁) h₂
                         ◃ (linvunitor
                              ((pr111 ...) e
                               · (pr111 ...) e)
                            ▹ # R
                                (equifier_cone_pr1 e)))
                        • ((# (id_psfunctor B₁) h₂
                            ◃ (((...) • (...))
                               ▹ # R
                                   (equifier_cone_pr1
                                      e)))
                           • ((# (id_psfunctor B₁) h₂
                               ◃ (invertible_modcomponent_of
                                    ... e ▹ # R ...))
                              • (# (id_psfunctor B₁)
                                   h₂
                                 ◃ lunitor (# R ...)))))))))))) =

                        • ((# (id_psfunctor B₁) h₂
                            ◃ (invertible_modcomponent_of
                                 (biadj_triangle_r R)
                                 e
                               ▹ # R
                                   (equifier_cone_pr1
                                      e)))
                           • (# (id_psfunctor B₁) h₂
                              ◃ lunitor
                                  (# R
                                     (equifier_cone_pr1
                                        e)))))))))))) =
(biadj_unit R x
 ◃ ((psfunctor_comp R (# L h₁)
       (biadj_counit (pr1 R) e)) ^-1
    ▹ # R (equifier_cone_pr1 e)))
• (lassociator (biadj_unit R x)
     (# R (# L h₁) · # R (biadj_counit (pr1 R) e))
     (# R (equifier_cone_pr1 e))
   • ((lassociator (biadj_unit R x) (# R (# L h₁))
         (# R (biadj_counit (pr1 R) e))
       ▹ # R (equifier_cone_pr1 e))
      • (((psnaturality_of (biadj_unit R) h₁
           ▹ # R (biadj_counit (pr1 R) e))
          ▹ # R (equifier_cone_pr1 e))
         • (rassociator
              (# (id_psfunctor B₁) h₁
               · biadj_unit R (R e))
              (# R (biadj_counit (pr1 R) e))
              (# R (equifier_cone_pr1 e))
            • (rassociator (# (id_psfunctor B₁) h₁)
                 (biadj_unit R (R e))
                 (# R (biadj_counit (pr1 R) e)
                  · # R (equifier_cone_pr1 e))
               • ((# (id_psfunctor B₁) h₁
                   ◃ lassociator
                       ((pr111 (Whiskering.right_whisker
                                  (pr1 R)
                                  (biadj_unit (pr1 R))))
                          e)
                       ((pr111 (Whiskering.left_whisker
                                  (pr1 R)
                                  (biadj_counit
                                     (pr1 R)))) e)
                       (# R (equifier_cone_pr1 e)))
                  • ((# (id_psfunctor B₁) h₁
                      ◃ (linvunitor
                           ((pr111 (Whiskering.right_whisker
                                      ... ...)) e
                            · (pr111 (Whiskering.left_whisker
                                        ... ...)) e)
                         ▹ # R (equifier_cone_pr1 e)))
                     • ((# (id_psfunctor B₁) h₁
                         ◃ (((id₁ ... ◃ (...))
                             • (id₁ ... ◃ (...)))
                            ▹ # R
                                (equifier_cone_pr1 e)))
                        • ((# (id_psfunctor B₁) h₁
                            ◃ (invertible_modcomponent_of
                                 (biadj_triangle_r R)
                                 e
                               ▹ # R
                                   (equifier_cone_pr1
                                      e)))
                           • ((# (id_psfunctor B₁) h₁
                               ◃ lunitor (# R ...))
                              • (ζ
                                 ▹ # R
                                     (equifier_cone_pr1
                                        e))))))))))))

      
B₁, B₂: bicat
L: psfunctor B₁ B₂
R: left_biadj_data L
y₁, y₂: B₂
f, g: B₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
α, β: f ==> g
e: equifier_cone f g α β
He: has_equifier_ump e
x: B₁
h₁, h₂: hom x (R e)
ζ: hom x (R e) ⟦ h₁, h₂ ⟧
(biadj_unit R x
 ◃ ((psfunctor_comp R (# L h₁) (biadj_counit R e)) ^-1
    ▹ # R (equifier_cone_pr1 e)))
• ((biadj_unit R x
    ◃ ((## R (## L ζ) ▹ # R (biadj_counit R e))
       ▹ # R (equifier_cone_pr1 e)))
   • (lassociator (biadj_unit R x)
        (# R (# L h₂) · # R (biadj_counit (pr1 R) e))
        (# R (equifier_cone_pr1 e))
      • ((lassociator (biadj_unit R x) (# R (# L h₂))
            (# R (biadj_counit (pr1 R) e))
          ▹ # R (equifier_cone_pr1 e))
         • (((psnaturality_of (biadj_unit R) h₂
              ▹ # R (biadj_counit (pr1 R) e))
             ▹ # R (equifier_cone_pr1 e))
            • (rassociator
                 (# (id_psfunctor B₁) h₂
                  · biadj_unit R (R e))
                 (# R (biadj_counit (pr1 R) e))
                 (# R (equifier_cone_pr1 e))
               • (rassociator (# (id_psfunctor B₁) h₂)
                    (biadj_unit R (R e))
                    (# R (biadj_counit (pr1 R) e)
                     · # R (equifier_cone_pr1 e))
                  • ((# (id_psfunctor B₁) h₂
                      ◃ lassociator
                          ((pr111 (Whiskering.right_whisker
                                     (pr1 R)
                                     (biadj_unit (...))))
                             e)
                          ((pr111 (Whiskering.left_whisker
                                     (pr1 R)
                                     (biadj_counit
                                        (...)))) e)
                          (# R (equifier_cone_pr1 e)))
                     • ((# (id_psfunctor B₁) h₂
                         ◃ (linvunitor
                              ((pr111 ...) e
                               · (pr111 ...) e)
                            ▹ # R
                                (equifier_cone_pr1 e)))
                        • ((# (id_psfunctor B₁) h₂
                            ◃ (((...) • (...))
                               ▹ # R
                                   (equifier_cone_pr1
                                      e)))
                           • ((# (id_psfunctor B₁) h₂
                               ◃ (invertible_modcomponent_of
                                    ... e ▹ # R ...))
                              • (# (id_psfunctor B₁)
                                   h₂
                                 ◃ lunitor (# R ...)))))))))))) =

                      ◃ (((id₁ (pr1 R e)
                           ◃ (... e ◃ linvunitor ...))
                          • (id₁ (pr1 R e)
                             ◃ (... e ◃ (...))))
                         ▹ # R (equifier_cone_pr1 e)))

                         ◃ (invertible_modcomponent_of
                              (biadj_triangle_r R) e
                            ▹ # R
                                (equifier_cone_pr1 e)))
                        • (# (id_psfunctor B₁) h₂
                           ◃ lunitor
                               (# R
                                  (equifier_cone_pr1 e))))))))))) =

                    ((pr111 (Whiskering.right_whisker
                               (pr1 R)
                               (biadj_unit (pr1 R))))
                       e)
                    ((pr111 (Whiskering.left_whisker
                               (pr1 R)
                               (biadj_counit (pr1 R))))
                       e) (# R (equifier_cone_pr1 e)))
               • ((# (id_psfunctor B₁) h₂
                   ◃ (linvunitor
                        ((pr111 (Whiskering.right_whisker
                                   (pr1 R)
                                   (biadj_unit ...)))
                           e
                         · (pr111 (Whiskering.left_whisker
                                     (pr1 R)
                                     (biadj_counit ...)))
                             e)
                      ▹ # R (equifier_cone_pr1 e)))
                  • ((# (id_psfunctor B₁) h₂
                      ◃ (((id₁ (pr1 R e)
                           ◃ (... e ◃ linvunitor ...))
                          • (id₁ (pr1 R e)
                             ◃ (... e ◃ (...))))
                         ▹ # R (equifier_cone_pr1 e)))
                     • ((# (id_psfunctor B₁) h₂
                         ◃ (invertible_modcomponent_of
                              (biadj_triangle_r R) e
                            ▹ # R
                                (equifier_cone_pr1 e)))
                        • (# (id_psfunctor B₁) h₂
                           ◃ lunitor
                               (# R
                                  (equifier_cone_pr1 e))))))))))) =

                     • (ζ ▹ # R (equifier_cone_pr1 e)))))))))

L: psfunctor B₁ B₂
R: left_biadj_data L
y₁, y₂: B₂

(((biadj_unit R x ◃ ## R (## L ζ))
  ▹ # R (biadj_counit (pr1 R) e))
 ▹ # R (equifier_cone_pr1 e))
• (((psnaturality_of (biadj_unit R) h₂
     ▹ # R (biadj_counit (pr1 R) e))
    ▹ # R (equifier_cone_pr1 e))
   • (rassociator
        (# (id_psfunctor B₁) h₂ · biadj_unit R (R e))
        (# R (biadj_counit (pr1 R) e))
        (# R (equifier_cone_pr1 e))
      • (rassociator (# (id_psfunctor B₁) h₂)
           (biadj_unit R (R e))
           (# R (biadj_counit (pr1 R) e)
            · # R (equifier_cone_pr1 e))
         • ((# (id_psfunctor B₁) h₂
             ◃ lassociator
                 ((pr111 (Whiskering.right_whisker
                            (pr1 R)
                            (biadj_unit (pr1 R)))) e)
                 ((pr111 (Whiskering.left_whisker
                            (pr1 R)
                            (biadj_counit (pr1 R)))) e)
                 (# R (equifier_cone_pr1 e)))
            • ((# (id_psfunctor B₁) h₂
                ◃ (linvunitor
                     ((pr111 (Whiskering.right_whisker
                                (pr1 R)
                                (biadj_unit (pr1 R))))
                        e
                      · (pr111 (Whiskering.left_whisker
                                  (pr1 R)
                                  (biadj_counit
                                     (pr1 R)))) e)
                   ▹ # R (equifier_cone_pr1 e)))
               • ((# (id_psfunctor B₁) h₂
                   ◃ (((id₁ (pr1 R e)
                        ◃ ((pr111 (...)) e
                           ◃ linvunitor (... e)))
                       • (id₁ (pr1 R e)
                          ◃ ((pr111 (...)) e
                             ◃ (id₁ ...
                                ◃ rinvunitor ...))))
                      ▹ # R (equifier_cone_pr1 e)))
                  • ((# (id_psfunctor B₁) h₂
                      ◃ (invertible_modcomponent_of
                           (biadj_triangle_r R) e
                         ▹ # R (equifier_cone_pr1 e)))
                     • (# (id_psfunctor B₁) h₂
                        ◃ lunitor
                            (# R (equifier_cone_pr1 e)))))))))) =
?b

     (# R (biadj_counit (pr1 R) e))
     (# R (equifier_cone_pr1 e))

        (biadj_unit R (R e))
        (# R (biadj_counit (pr1 R) e)
         · # R (equifier_cone_pr1 e))
      • ((# (id_psfunctor B₁) h₁
          ◃ lassociator
              ((pr111 (Whiskering.right_whisker
                         (pr1 R) (biadj_unit (pr1 R))))
                 e)
              ((pr111 (Whiskering.left_whisker (pr1 R)
                         (biadj_counit (pr1 R)))) e)
              (# R (equifier_cone_pr1 e)))
         • ((# (id_psfunctor B₁) h₁
             ◃ (linvunitor
                  ((pr111 (Whiskering.right_whisker
                             (pr1 R)
                             (biadj_unit (pr1 R)))) e
                   · (pr111 (Whiskering.left_whisker
                               (pr1 R)
                               (biadj_counit (pr1 R))))
                       e) ▹ # R (equifier_cone_pr1 e)))
            • ((# (id_psfunctor B₁) h₁
                ◃ (((id₁ (pr1 R e)
                     ◃ ((pr111 (Whiskering.right_whisker
                                  (...) (...))) e
                        ◃ linvunitor ((pr111 (...)) e)))
                    • (id₁ (pr1 R e)
                       ◃ ((pr111 (Whiskering.right_whisker
                                    (...) (...))) e
                          ◃ (id₁ (... e)
                             ◃ rinvunitor (... e)))))
                   ▹ # R (equifier_cone_pr1 e)))

                        (biadj_triangle_r R) e
                      ▹ # R (equifier_cone_pr1 e)))
                  • ((# (id_psfunctor B₁) h₁
                      ◃ lunitor
                          (# R (equifier_cone_pr1 e)))
                     • (ζ ▹ # R (equifier_cone_pr1 e)))))))))

                           (biadj_counit (pr1 R)))) e)))

      · (id₁

                      (comp_psfunctor (pr1 R) L)

      ◃ lunitor (# R (equifier_cone_pr1 e)))) =

 ◃ (invertible_modcomponent_of (biadj_triangle_r R) e

L: psfunctor B₁ B₂
R: left_biadj_data L
y₁, y₂: B₂
f, g: B₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
α, β: f ==> g
e: equifier_cone f g α β
He: has_equifier_ump e
x: B₁
(biadj_left_hom R x e
 ∙ to_universal_equifier_cat e (L x))
∙ full_sub_category_functor
    (λ h : hom (L x) y₁,
     make_hProp (h ◃ α = h ◃ β)
       (cellset_property (h · f) (h · g) (h ◃ α)
          (h ◃ β)))
    (λ h : hom x (R y₁),
     make_hProp (h ◃ ## R α = h ◃ ## R β)
       (cellset_property (h · # R f) (h · # R g)
          (h ◃ ## R α) (h ◃ ## R β)))
    (biadj_right_hom R x y₁) preserve_equifiers_R_path
⟹ to_universal_equifier_cat
    (psfunctor_equifier_cone R e) x

B₁, B₂: bicat
L: psfunctor B₁ B₂
R: left_biadj_data L
y₁, y₂: B₂
f, g: B₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
α, β: f ==> g
e: equifier_cone f g α β
He: has_equifier_ump e
x: B₁
h: hom x (R e)
is_invertible_2cell
  (((((((biadj_unit R x
         ◃ ((psfunctor_comp R
               (# L h · biadj_counit (pr1 R) e)
               (equifier_cone_pr1 e)) ^-1
            • ((psfunctor_comp R (# L h)
                  (biadj_counit (pr1 R) e)) ^-1
               ▹ # R (equifier_cone_pr1 e))))
        • lassociator (biadj_unit R x)
            (# R (# L h)
             · # R (biadj_counit (pr1 R) e))
            (# R (equifier_cone_pr1 e)))
       • (lassociator (biadj_unit R x) (# R (# L h))
            (# R (biadj_counit (pr1 R) e))
          ▹ # R (equifier_cone_pr1 e)))
      • ((psnaturality_of (biadj_unit R) h
          ▹ # R (biadj_counit (pr1 R) e))
         ▹ # R (equifier_cone_pr1 e)))
     • rassociator
         (# (id_psfunctor B₁) h · biadj_unit R (R e))
         (# R (biadj_counit (pr1 R) e))
         (# R (equifier_cone_pr1 e)))
    • rassociator (# (id_psfunctor B₁) h)
        (biadj_unit R (R e))
        (# R (biadj_counit (pr1 R) e)
         · # R (equifier_cone_pr1 e)))
   • (# (id_psfunctor B₁) h
      ◃ ((lassociator
            ((pr111 (Whiskering.right_whisker (pr1 R)
                       (biadj_unit (pr1 R)))) e)
            ((pr111 (Whiskering.left_whisker (pr1 R)
                       (biadj_counit (pr1 R)))) e)
            (# R (equifier_cone_pr1 e))
          • (((linvunitor
                 ((pr111 (Whiskering.right_whisker
                            (pr1 R)
                            (biadj_unit (pr1 R)))) e
                  · (pr111 (Whiskering.left_whisker
                              (pr1 R)
                              (biadj_counit (pr1 R))))
                      e)
               • (id₁ (pr1 R e)
                  ◃ ((pr111 (Whiskering.right_whisker
                               (pr1 R)
                               (biadj_unit (pr1 R))))
                       e
                     ◃ (linvunitor
                          ((pr111 (Whiskering.left_whisker
                                     ... ...)) e)
                        • (id₁ ((pr111 ...) e)
                           ◃ rinvunitor
                               ((pr111 ...) e))))))
              • invertible_modcomponent_of
                  (biadj_triangle_r R) e)
             ▹ # R (equifier_cone_pr1 e)))
         • lunitor (# R (equifier_cone_pr1 e)))))

# L h ◃ (## L (## R β) ▹ biadj_counit R y₂)

      
B₁, B₂: bicat
L: psfunctor B₁ B₂
R: left_biadj_data L
y₁, y₂: B₂
f, g: B₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
α, β: f ==> g
e: equifier_cone f g α β
He: has_equifier_ump e
x: B₁
h: B₁ ⟦ x, R y₁ ⟧
p: h ◃ ## R α = h ◃ ## R β
q: # L h ◃ ## L (## R α) = # L h ◃ ## L (## R β)
is_invertible_2cell
  (lassociator (# L h) (# L (# R g))
     (biadj_counit R y₂))
B₁, B₂: bicat
L: psfunctor B₁ B₂
R: left_biadj_data L
y₁, y₂: B₂
f, g: B₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
α, β: f ==> g
e: equifier_cone f g α β
He: has_equifier_ump e
x: B₁
h: B₁ ⟦ x, R y₁ ⟧
p: h ◃ ## R α = h ◃ ## R β
q: # L h ◃ ## L (## R α) = # L h ◃ ## L (## R β)
(# L h ◃ (## L (## R α) ▹ biadj_counit R y₂))
• lassociator (# L h) (# L (# R g))
    (biadj_counit R y₂) =
(# L h ◃ (## L (## R β) ▹ biadj_counit R y₂))
• lassociator (# L h) (# L (# R g))
    (biadj_counit R y₂)

      
B₁, B₂: bicat
L: psfunctor B₁ B₂
R: left_biadj_data L
y₁, y₂: B₂
f, g: B₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
α, β: f ==> g
e: equifier_cone f g α β
He: has_equifier_ump e
x: B₁
h: B₁ ⟦ x, R y₁ ⟧
p: h ◃ ## R α = h ◃ ## R β
q: # L h ◃ ## L (## R α) = # L h ◃ ## L (## R β)
is_invertible_2cell
  (lassociator (# L h) (# L (# R g))
     (biadj_counit R y₂))

        is_iso.
      
B₁, B₂: bicat
L: psfunctor B₁ B₂
R: left_biadj_data L
y₁, y₂: B₂
f, g: B₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
α, β: f ==> g
e: equifier_cone f g α β
He: has_equifier_ump e
x: B₁
h: B₁ ⟦ x, R y₁ ⟧
p: h ◃ ## R α = h ◃ ## R β
q: # L h ◃ ## L (## R α) = # L h ◃ ## L (## R β)
(# L h ◃ (## L (## R α) ▹ biadj_counit R y₂))
• lassociator (# L h) (# L (# R g))
    (biadj_counit R y₂) =
(# L h ◃ (## L (## R β) ▹ biadj_counit R y₂))
• lassociator (# L h) (# L (# R g))
    (biadj_counit R y₂)

      
B₁, B₂: bicat
L: psfunctor B₁ B₂
R: left_biadj_data L
y₁, y₂: B₂
f, g: B₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
α, β: f ==> g
e: equifier_cone f g α β
He: has_equifier_ump e
x: B₁
h: B₁ ⟦ x, R y₁ ⟧
p: h ◃ ## R α = h ◃ ## R β
q: # L h ◃ ## L (## R α) = # L h ◃ ## L (## R β)
lassociator (# L h) (# L (# R f)) (biadj_counit R y₂)
• ((# L h ◃ ## L (## R α)) ▹ biadj_counit R y₂) =
lassociator (# L h) (# L (# R f)) (biadj_counit R y₂)
• ((# L h ◃ ## L (## R β)) ▹ biadj_counit R y₂)

      
B₁, B₂: bicat
L: psfunctor B₁ B₂
R: left_biadj_data L
y₁, y₂: B₂
f, g: B₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
α, β: f ==> g
e: equifier_cone f g α β
He: has_equifier_ump e
x: B₁
h: B₁ ⟦ x, R y₁ ⟧
p: h ◃ ## R α = h ◃ ## R β
q: # L h ◃ ## L (## R α) = # L h ◃ ## L (## R β)
# L h ◃ ## L (## R α) = # L h ◃ ## L (## R β)

      exact q.
    Qed.
  End PreserveEquifiers.

R: left_biadj_data L
HB₁: is_univalent_2_1 B₁
HB₂: is_univalent_2_1 B₂

f, g: B₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
α, β: f ==> g
e: equifier_cone f g α β
He: has_equifier_ump e
x: B₁
hom x (psfunctor_equifier_cone R e)
⟶ universal_equifier_cat x
 exact (biadj_left_hom R x e
             ∙ to_universal_equifier_cat e (L x)
             ∙ full_sub_category_functor
                 (λ (h : hom (L x) y₁),
                  make_hProp
                    (h ◃ α = h ◃ β)
                    (cellset_property _ _ _ _))
                 (λ (h : hom x (R y₁)),
                  make_hProp
                    (h ◃ ## R α = h ◃ ## R β)
                    (cellset_property _ _ _ _))
                 (biadj_right_hom R x y₁)
                 preserve_equifiers_R_path).
    
B₁, B₂: bicat
L: psfunctor B₁ B₂
R: left_biadj_data L
HB₁: is_univalent_2_1 B₁
HB₂: is_univalent_2_1 B₂

f, g: B₂ ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧

He: has_equifier_ump e
x: B₁
(biadj_left_hom R x e
 ∙ to_universal_equifier_cat e (L x))
∙ full_sub_category_functor
    (λ h : hom (L x) y₁,
     make_hProp (h ◃ α = h ◃ β)
       (cellset_property (h · f) (h · g) (h ◃ α)
          (h ◃ β)))
    (λ h : hom x (R y₁),
     make_hProp (h ◃ ## R α = h ◃ ## R β)
       (cellset_property (h · # R f) (h · # R g)
          (h ◃ ## R α) (h ◃ ## R β)))
    (biadj_right_hom R x y₁) preserve_equifiers_R_path
⟹ to_universal_equifier_cat
    (psfunctor_equifier_cone R e) x
 exact (right_biadj_preserves_equifiers_commute x).

x: B₁
∏ x0 : hom x (R y₁),
(λ h : hom x (R y₁),
 make_hProp (h ◃ ## R α = h ◃ ## R β)
   (cellset_property (h · # R f) (h · # R g)
      (h ◃ ## R α) (h ◃ ## R β))) x0
→ (λ h : hom (L x) y₁,
   make_hProp (h ◃ α = h ◃ β)
     (cellset_property (h · f) (h · g) (h ◃ α) (h ◃ β)))
    (right_adjoint ?L_equiv x0)
